<Time>1400426503836<//Time>< Review>
For most people going to Isabella, Kernville, Wofford Heights, etc. this place could be most useful for the camping selections. Many basics and some things you may have never known about. Also the employees will help you, if you ask for it, otherwise you get a friendly greeting and "unbothered" shopping.  The section for work clothes is also vast, working up the canyon, this was my first place to go to get work clothes. (Beats waiting about a week for UPS to find me). Overall, fair to low prices, friendly staff, and neat and clean location, even if you don't 'need' surplus... Stop in and take a look around.</Review>

< Review>
Sensational free tour of the dam tunnel and generators is available. Pick up tickets at visitors centre. Security is tight. If you are interested in how the dam was constructed and hydro-electric generation then you will enjoy this. You need to be able to walk to the centre of the dam wall to start the indoor tour. Afterward watch the free video in the visitors centre.< /Review>

<date>1576067254298<//date><rating>4< /rating><review>I have been to this restaurant 3 times so far and am a big fan!

THE FOOD: Is delicious and made fresh.  I am Filipino and am so happy to see a that serves authentic Filipino food thriving.  There is a lot of variety on their menu and the lunch buffet cannot be beat!  If you order off the regular menu the portions are HUGE!  Definitely enough to share between 4 people or take home.

THE SERVICE: Is good.  The food comes out pretty quickly and the servers are there if you need anything.

THE AMBIANCE: Is pretty cool.  I really enjoy the outdoor patio area.  The greenery makes it feel like you are in the middle of the Arts District and is pretty peaceful...as long as there are no noisy cars outside.

THE BUFFET: Is worth it.  It's truly $10 for all you can eat.  Some items in the buffet rotate so I would call ahead to check in if there is something specific you are looking for.  They always have rice, pancit, fried chicken and lumpia.

OVERALL: I am looking forward to going back.  I have already taken friends here during the lunch buffet and at dinner.  I love exposing my friends to new types of food and am happy they were able to taste a little bit of my culture.  It's a great spot and if you aren't sure where to start I would go to the lunch buffet. Enjoy! Salamat!<//review><Pics>None< /Pics><resp>None</resp>< gmap_id>
